style=\"margin: 5px -40px 15px 0px; color: rgb(85, 85, 85); font-size: 21px; padding-left:0px\">Online Banking Security</h2>\n<div class=\"lineAngleDiv\" style=\"margin-top: 0px;\"></div> \n<h3>Secure home page sign in</h3>\n<p> Those who become a part of Meriwest enjoy the security of banking with a financial institution that's established, financially sound and has a strong local heritage.</p><p>Ensuring the security of your personal information online is a top priority for us. When you sign in to Online Banking, your account number and password are always secure. With our multi-factor authentication you  have an extra layer of security working behind-the-scenes to protect your account. This means you can  bank online with a renewed sense of confidence and security. \n</p>\n<p> <a class=\"insidelink\" href=\"security\"><strong>Learn more about your online banking security</strong></a></p>\n<div class=\"lineAngleDiv\"></div> \n<h3>Browser security indicators</h3>\nYou may notice when you are on our home page that some familiar indicators do not appear in your browser to confirm the entire page is secure. Those indicators include the small \"lock\" icon in the bottom right corner of the browser frame and the \"s\" in the Web address bar (for example, \"https\").<p></p><div class=\"lineAngleDiv\"></div> \n\n<h3>We help keep your personal and financial information protected</h3>\nThe number of people who may become victims of identity theft is on the increase as more consumers make use of electronic means to purchase products and pay debts.<br><br>\nAt Meriwest Credit Union, keeping your personal and financial information secure is one of our highest priorities and most important responsibilities. You should feel safe knowing we will work with you to prevent fraud and identity theft. And, in the situation that something should happen, we will help you resolve it as quickly and easily as possible. \n<strong><a class=\"insidelink\" href=\"/rcfs/yourpdfs/marketing/meriwest_consumer_awareness_personal_financial_info.pdf\" target=\"_new\">This document will help you take steps to better understand and protect your personal and financial information</a></strong>.<p></p>\n\n<p>For answers to any other online security questions please refer to our <a class=\"insidelink\" href=\"onlinefaqs\"><strong>Frequently Asked Questions section</strong></a>.</p>\n\n<p>Find out more about protecting your personal security and banking experience by reading the <a class=\"insidelink\" href=\"phishing\"><strong>Basics on Phishing</strong></a>.</p><div class=\"lineAngleDiv\"></div>\n  <div class=\"insidePageBox\" style=\"background-color: rgb(249, 249, 249);\"> <div class=\"row\" style=\"padding: 10px;\"> <div 321176833&lt;/strong&gt;. &amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p&gt;Routing numbers identify the financial institution from and to which funds are transferred. This number allows companies and individuals to know which specific bank, out of all banks, has the account in question.&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt; A routing number comes in the form of a nine-digit number that usually precedes the account number found at the bottom portion of checks.&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt; Financial institutions use routing numbers in order to process payments electronically. 321176833&lt;/strong&gt;. &amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;\n&lt;p&gt;Routing numbers identify the financial institution from and to which funds are transferred. This number allows companies and individuals to know which specific bank, out of all banks, has the account in question.&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt; A routing number comes in the form of a nine-digit number that usually precedes the account number found at the bottom portion of checks.&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt; Financial institutions use routing numbers in order to process payments electronically. information online is a top priority for us. When you sign in to Online Banking, your account number and password are always secure. With our multi-factor authentication you now have an extra layer of security working behind-the-scenes to protect your account. This means you can now bank online with a renewed sense of confidence and security. </p><p> By employing multi-factor authentication, Meriwest Credit Union can lessen vulnerabilities in the account opening process, making it more difficult for those with fraudulent intent to access our financial system and your account. Here at Meriwest Credit Union, we use an automated system to validate and verify a members identifying information. This is a highly effective means of mitigating fraud risk and protecting your accounts. Go to our<strong> <a class=\"insidelink\" href=\"https://meriwestonline.meriwest.com/Banking/\">secure login page</a></strong>.</p>\n<div class=\"lineAngleDiv\"></div> \n<h3>Browser security indicators</h3><p>\nYou may notice when you are on our home page that some familiar indicators do not appear in your browser to confirm the entire page is secure. Those indicators include the small \"lock\" icon in the bottom right corner of the browser frame and the \"s\" in the Web address bar (for example, \"https\").</p><div class=\"lineAngleDiv\"></div> \n\n<h3>Meriwest Credit Union helps keep your personal and financial information protected</h3>\n<p>The number of people who may become victims of identity theft is on the increase as more consumers make use of electronic means to purchase products and pay debts.</p><p>\nAt Meriwest Credit Union, keeping your personal and financial information secure is one of our highest priorities and most important responsibilities. You should feel safe knowing we will work with you to prevent fraud and identity theft.
